<p><strong>Features</strong></p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Automatically focuses the next field on typing and focuses the previous field
on deletion</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports numeric and alphanumeric values</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports masking value (for sensitive data)</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports copy/paste to autofill all fields</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted">Supports fast paste SMS-code</li>
</ul>

<h2 id="anatomy" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Anatomy<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#anatomy"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Check the pin input anatomy and part names.</p>

<h2 id="usage" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Usage<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#usage"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Import the pin input package:</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword module">import</span> <span class="token imports"><span class="token operator">*</span> <span class="token keyword module">as</span> pinInput</span> <span class="token keyword module">from</span> <span class="token string">&quot;@zag-js/pin-input&quot;</span>
</span></div></pre>
<p>These are the key exports:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">machine</code> - State machine logic.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">connect</code> - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.</li>
</ul>
<blockquote class="my_5 px_4 py_3 bg_bg.tertiary.subtle bd-w_1px bd-l-c_border.primary.subtle bd-l-w_2px bdr_4px bd-c_border">
<p>You&#x27;ll need to provide a unique <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">id</code> to the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">useMachine</code> hook. This is used to
ensure every part has a unique identifier.</p>
</blockquote>
<p>Then use the framework integration helpers:</p>

<h3 id="setting-a-default-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting a default value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-a-default-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">defaultValue</code> to define the initial pin value. It must be an array of
strings.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">defaultValue</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token string">&quot;1&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;2&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token string">&quot;&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="controlled-value" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Controlled value<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#controlled-value"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">value</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> properties to programmatically control the
value of the pin input.</p>

<h3 id="setting-input-count" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Setting input count<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#setting-input-count"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">count</code> to define the number of input fields to render.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">count</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">6</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="changing-the-placeholder" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Changing the placeholder<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#changing-the-placeholder"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To customize the default pin input placeholder (○) for each input, pass the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">placeholder</code> prop and set it to your desired value.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">placeholder</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;*&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="blur-on-complete" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Blur on complete<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#blur-on-complete"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the last input maintains focus when filled and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueComplete</code> is
invoked. To blur the last input when the user completes the input, set the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">blurOnComplete: true</code> in the machine&#x27;s context.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">blurOnComplete</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="allowing-alphanumeric-values" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Allowing alphanumeric values<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#allowing-alphanumeric-values"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>By default, the pin input accepts only number values but you can choose between
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">numeric</code>, <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">alphanumeric</code> and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">alphabetic</code> values. To change the input mode,
pass the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">type</code> context property and set its value to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">alphanumeric</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">type</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;alphanumeric&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="using-otp-mode" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Using OTP mode<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#using-otp-mode"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>To trigger smartphone OTP auto-suggestion, it is recommended to set the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autocomplete</code> attribute to &quot;one-time-code&quot;. The pin-input machine provides
support for this automatically when you set the <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">otp</code> context property to
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">otp</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="securing-the-text-input" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Securing the text input<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#securing-the-text-input"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When collecting private or sensitive information using the pin input, you might
need to mask the value entered, similar to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">&lt;input type=&quot;password&quot;/&gt;</code>. Pass the
<code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">mask</code> context property and set it to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">true</code>.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">mask</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="listening-for-changes" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Listening for changes<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#listening-for-changes"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The pin input machine invokes several callback functions when the user enters:</p>
<ul>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueChange</code> — Function invoked when the value is changed.</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueComplete</code> — Function invoked when all fields have been completed (by
typing or pasting).</li>
<li class="[&amp;::marker]:c_text.muted"><code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">onValueInvalid</code> — Function invoked when an invalid value is entered into the
input. An invalid value is any value that doesn&#x27;t match the specified &quot;type&quot;.</li>
</ul>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueChange</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string[], valueAsString: string }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;value changed to:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">value</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueComplete</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { value: string[], valueAsString: string }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;completed value:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token function">onValueInvalid</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">details</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token comment">// details =&gt; { index: number, value: string }</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token console class-name">console</span><span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token method function property-access">log</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token string">&quot;invalid value:&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> details<span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="autofocus-and-selection-behavior" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Autofocus and selection behavior<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#autofocus-and-selection-behavior"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">autoFocus</code> to focus the first input on mount, and <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">selectOnFocus</code> to select
the active character on focus.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">autoFocus</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">selectOnFocus</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token boolean">true</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="rtl-support" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">RTL support<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#rtl-support"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The pin input machine supports RTL writing directions. Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code> to <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">rtl</code>.</p>
<p>When this attribute is set, we attach a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">dir</code> attribute to the root part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line highlight-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">dir</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;rtl&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="submitting-with-an-external-form" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Submitting with an external form<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#submitting-with-an-external-form"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Set <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code> if the hidden input should submit with a form outside the current DOM
subtree.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">name</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;value&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">form</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token string">&quot;checkout-form&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="customizing-accessibility-labels" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Customizing accessibility labels<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#customizing-accessibility-labels"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>Use <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">translations.inputLabel</code> to customize screen-reader labels per input.</p>
<pre class="prose language-jsx"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token keyword">const</span> service <span class="token operator">=</span> <span class="token function">useMachine</span><span class="token punctuation">(</span>pinInput<span class="token punctuation">.</span><span class="token property-access">machine</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">count</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token number">4</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token literal-property property">translations</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">    <span class="token function-variable function">inputLabel</span><span class="token operator">:</span> <span class="token punctuation">(</span><span class="token parameter">index<span class="token punctuation">,</span> length</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span> <span class="token arrow operator">=&gt;</span> <span class="token template-string"><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span><span class="token string">Digit </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>index <span class="token operator">+</span> <span class="token number">1</span><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token string"> of </span><span class="token interpolation"><span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">${</span>length<span class="token interpolation-punctuation punctuation">}</span></span><span class="token template-punctuation string">`</span></span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">,</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span><span class="token punctuation">)</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="styling-guide" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Styling guide<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#styling-guide"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<p>Each part includes a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-part</code> attribute you can target in CSS.</p>
<h3 id="completed-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Completed state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#completed-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When all values have been filled, we attach a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-complete</code> attribute to the
root and input parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-complete</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when all value has been filled */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-complete</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when all value has been filled */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="invalid-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Invalid state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#invalid-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When an invalid value is entered, we attach a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-invalid</code> attribute to the
affected input part.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-invalid</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the input is invalid */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h3 id="disabled-state" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Disabled state<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#disabled-state"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>When the pin-input is disabled, we attach a <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">data-disabled</code> attribute to the
root and input parts.</p>
<pre class="prose language-css"><div class="prose"><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;root&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the input is disabled */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span><span class="code-line">
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token selector"><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-part</span><span class="token operator">=</span><span class="token attr-value">&quot;input&quot;</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span><span class="token attribute"><span class="token punctuation">[</span><span class="token attr-name">data-disabled</span><span class="token punctuation">]</span></span></span> <span class="token punctuation">{</span>
</span><span class="code-line">  <span class="token comment">/* styles for when the input is disabled */</span>
</span><span class="code-line"><span class="token punctuation">}</span>
</span></div></pre>
<h2 id="methods-and-properties" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Methods and Properties<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#methods-and-properties"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="machine-context" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine Context<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-context"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The pin input machine exposes the following context properties:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">name</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The name of the input element. Useful for form submission.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">form</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The associate form of the underlying input element.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">pattern</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The regular expression that the user-entered input value is checked against.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">ids</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">Partial&lt;{ root: string; hiddenInput: string; label: string; control: string; input: (id: string) =&gt; string; }&gt;</code><span class="d_block">The ids of the elements in the pin input. Useful for composition.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono <h3 id="machine-api" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Machine API<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#machine-api"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<p>The pin input <code class="white-space_nowrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">api</code> exposes the following methods:</p>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_0 pl_0! li-t_none dvd-y_1px li-pos_inside"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">valueAsString</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">string</code><span class="d_block">The value of the input as a string.</span></li><li prose">complete</code><code class="fs_sm white-space_pre-wrap">boolean</code><span class="d_block">Whether all inputs are filled.</span></li><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_6"><code class="white-space_pre-wrap bg_bg.code.inline bdr_3px py_0.1em px_0.4em mx_0.1em fs_0.84em ff_mono fw_semibold c_pink.600 dark:c_pink.400 prose">count</code><code class="fs_sm <h2 id="accessibility" class="textStyle_display.md mt_12 mb_3">Accessibility<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#accessibility"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h2>
<h3 id="keyboard-interactions" class="textStyle_display.sm mt_6 mb_4">Keyboard Interactions<a class="c_green.500 cursor_pointer fw_medium td_underline td-c_cyan.default td-t_1px tu-o_2px hover:td-t_2px anchor" href="#keyboard-interactions"><span class="icon icon-link"></span></a></h3>
<ul class="d_flex flex-d_column gap_8px pl_0! li-t_none li-pos_inside dvd-y_1px"><li class="d_flex flex-d_column ai_flex-start gap_2 py_4"><div class="d_flex ai_center gap_8px flex-d_row"><kbd pin input is optimized for entering a sequence of digits or letters. The\ninput fields allow one character at a time. When the digit or letter is entered,\nfocus transfers to the next input in the sequence, until every input is filled.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cresources pkg=\"@zag-js/pin-input\"\u003e\n\u003cshowcase id=\"PinInput\"\u003e\n\u003cp\u003e\u003cstrong\u003eFeatures\u003c/strong\u003e\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eAutomatically focuses the next field on typing and focuses the previous field\non deletion\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports numeric and alphanumeric values\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports masking value (for sensitive data)\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports copy/paste to autofill all fields\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003eSupports fast paste SMS-code\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eInstallation\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eInstall the pin input package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"pin-input/installation.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eAnatomy\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eCheck the pin input anatomy and part names.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a \u003ccode\u003edata-part\u003c/code\u003e attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003canatomy id=\"pin-input\"\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eUsage\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eImport the pin input package:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003eimport * as pinInput from \"@zag-js/pin-input\"\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThese are the key exports:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003emachine\u003c/code\u003e - State machine logic.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003econnect\u003c/code\u003e - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cblockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eYou'll need to provide a unique \u003ccode\u003eid\u003c/code\u003e to the \u003ccode\u003euseMachine\u003c/code\u003e hook. This is used to\nensure every part has a unique identifier.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003c/blockquote\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThen use the framework integration helpers:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"pin-input/usage.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting a default value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003edefaultValue\u003c/code\u003e to define the initial pin value. It must be an array of\nstrings.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [\"1\", \"2\", \"\"],\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eControlled value\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse the \u003ccode\u003evalue\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e properties to programmatically control the\nvalue of the pin input.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003ccodesnippet id=\"pin-input/controlled.mdx\"\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSetting input count\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003ecount\u003c/code\u003e to define the number of input fields to render.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  count: 6,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eChanging the placeholder\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo customize the default pin input placeholder (○) for each input, pass the\n\u003ccode\u003eplaceholder\u003c/code\u003e prop and set it to your desired value.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  placeholder: \"*\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eBlur on complete\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the last input maintains focus when filled and \u003ccode\u003eonValueComplete\u003c/code\u003e is\ninvoked. To blur the last input when the user completes the input, set the\n\u003ccode\u003eblurOnComplete: true\u003c/code\u003e in the machine's context.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  blurOnComplete: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAllowing alphanumeric values\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eBy default, the pin input accepts only number values but you can choose between\n\u003ccode\u003enumeric\u003c/code\u003e, \u003ccode\u003ealphanumeric\u003c/code\u003e and \u003ccode\u003ealphabetic\u003c/code\u003e values. To change the input mode,\npass the \u003ccode\u003etype\u003c/code\u003e context property and set its value to \u003ccode\u003ealphanumeric\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  type: \"alphanumeric\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eUsing OTP mode\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eTo trigger smartphone OTP auto-suggestion, it is recommended to set the\n\u003ccode\u003eautocomplete\u003c/code\u003e attribute to \"one-time-code\". The pin-input machine provides\nsupport for this automatically when you set the \u003ccode\u003eotp\u003c/code\u003e context property to\n\u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  otp: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSecuring the text input\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen collecting private or sensitive information using the pin input, you might\nneed to mask the value entered, similar to \u003ccode\u003e\u0026#x3C;input type=\"password\"/\u003e\u003c/code\u003e. Pass the\n\u003ccode\u003emask\u003c/code\u003e context property and set it to \u003ccode\u003etrue\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  mask: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eListening for changes\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe pin input machine invokes several callback functions when the user enters:\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cul\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonValueChange\u003c/code\u003e — Function invoked when the value is changed.\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonValueComplete\u003c/code\u003e — Function invoked when all fields have been completed (by\ntyping or pasting).\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003cli\u003e\u003ccode\u003eonValueInvalid\u003c/code\u003e — Function invoked when an invalid value is entered into the\ninput. An invalid value is any value that doesn't match the specified \"type\".\u003c/li\u003e\n\u003c/ul\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[], valueAsString: string }\n    console.log(\"value changed to:\", details.value)\n  },\n  onValueComplete(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[], valueAsString: string }\n    console.log(\"completed value:\", details)\n  },\n  onValueInvalid(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { index: number, value: string }\n    console.log(\"invalid value:\", details)\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eAutofocus and selection behavior\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003eautoFocus\u003c/code\u003e to focus the first input on mount, and \u003ccode\u003eselectOnFocus\u003c/code\u003e to select\nthe active character on focus.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  autoFocus: true,\n  selectOnFocus: true,\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eRTL support\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eThe pin input machine supports RTL writing directions. Set \u003ccode\u003edir\u003c/code\u003e to \u003ccode\u003ertl\u003c/code\u003e.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen this attribute is set, we attach a \u003ccode\u003edir\u003c/code\u003e attribute to the root part.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\" metastring=\"{2}\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  dir: \"rtl\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eSubmitting with an external form\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eSet \u003ccode\u003eform\u003c/code\u003e if the hidden input should submit with a form outside the current DOM\nsubtree.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  name: \"value\",\n  form: \"checkout-form\",\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eCustomizing accessibility labels\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eUse \u003ccode\u003etranslations.inputLabel\u003c/code\u003e to customize screen-reader labels per input.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-jsx\"\u003econst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  count: 4,\n  translations: {\n    inputLabel: (index, length) =\u003e `Digit ${index + 1} of ${length}`,\n  },\n})\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch2\u003eStyling guide\u003c/h2\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eEach part includes a */\n}\n\u003c/code\u003e\u003c/pre\u003e\n\u003ch3\u003eInvalid state\u003c/h3\u003e\n\u003cp\u003eWhen an invalid value is entered, we attach a \u003ccode\u003edata-invalid\u003c/code\u003e attribute to the\naffected input part.\u003c/p\u003e\n\u003cpre\u003e\u003ccode class=\"language-css\"\u003e[data-part=\"input\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for when the input is invalid digits or letters. The\ninput fields allow one character at a time. When the digit or letter is entered,\nfocus transfers to the next input in the sequence, until every input is filled.\n\n\u003cResources pkg=\"@zag-js/pin-input\" /\u003e\n\n\u003cShowcase id=\"PinInput\" /\u003e\n\n**Features**\n\n- Automatically focuses the next field on typing and focuses the previous field\n  on deletion\n- Supports numeric and alphanumeric values\n- Supports masking value (for sensitive data)\n- Supports copy/paste to autofill all fields\n- Supports fast paste SMS-code\n\n## Installation\n\nInstall the pin input package:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"pin-input/installation.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n## Anatomy\n\nCheck the pin input anatomy and part names.\n\n\u003e Each part includes a `data-part` attribute to help identify them in the DOM.\n\n\u003cAnatomy id=\"pin-input\" /\u003e\n\n## Usage\n\nImport the pin input package:\n\n```jsx\nimport * as pinInput from \"@zag-js/pin-input\"\n```\n\nThese are the key exports:\n\n- `machine` - State machine logic.\n- `connect` - Maps machine state to JSX props and event handlers.\n\n\u003e You'll need to provide a unique `id` to the `useMachine` hook. This is used to\n\u003e ensure every part has a unique identifier.\n\nThen use the framework integration helpers:\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"pin-input/usage.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting a default value\n\nSet `defaultValue` to define the initial pin value. It must be an array of\nstrings.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  defaultValue: [\"1\", \"2\", \"\"],\n})\n```\n\n### Controlled value\n\nUse the `value` and `onValueChange` properties to programmatically control the\nvalue of the pin input.\n\n\u003cCodeSnippet id=\"pin-input/controlled.mdx\" /\u003e\n\n### Setting input count\n\nSet `count` to define the number of input fields to render.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  count: 6,\n})\n```\n\n### Changing the placeholder\n\nTo customize the default pin input placeholder (○) for each input, pass the\n`placeholder` prop and set it to your desired value.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  placeholder: \"*\",\n})\n```\n\n### Blur on complete\n\nBy default, the last input maintains focus when filled and `onValueComplete` is\ninvoked. To blur the last input when the user completes the input, set the\n`blurOnComplete: true` in the machine's context.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  blurOnComplete: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Allowing alphanumeric values\n\nBy default, the pin input accepts only number values but you can choose between\n`numeric`, `alphanumeric` and `alphabetic` values. To change the input mode,\npass the `type` context property and set its value to `alphanumeric`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  type: \"alphanumeric\",\n})\n```\n\n### Using OTP mode\n\nTo trigger smartphone OTP auto-suggestion, it is recommended to set the\n`autocomplete` attribute to \"one-time-code\". The pin-input machine provides\nsupport for this automatically when you set the `otp` context property to\n`true`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  otp: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Securing the text input\n\nWhen collecting private or sensitive information using the pin input, you might\nneed to mask the value entered, similar to `\u003cinput type=\"password\"/\u003e`. Pass the\n`mask` context property and set it to `true`.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  mask: true,\n})\n```\n\n### Listening for changes\n\nThe pin input machine invokes several callback functions when the user enters:\n\n- `onValueChange` — Function invoked when the value is changed.\n- `onValueComplete` — Function invoked when all fields have been completed (by\n  typing or pasting).\n- `onValueInvalid` — Function invoked when an invalid value is entered into the\n  input. An invalid value is any value that doesn't match the specified \"type\".\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  onValueChange(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[], valueAsString: string }\n    console.log(\"value changed to:\", details.value)\n  },\n  onValueComplete(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { value: string[], valueAsString: string }\n    console.log(\"completed value:\", details)\n  },\n  onValueInvalid(details) {\n    // details =\u003e { index: number, value: string }\n    console.log(\"invalid value:\", details)\n  },\n})\n```\n\n### Autofocus and selection behavior\n\nUse `autoFocus` to focus the first input on mount, and `selectOnFocus` to select\nthe active character on focus.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  autoFocus: true,\n  selectOnFocus: true,\n})\n```\n\n### RTL support\n\nThe pin input machine supports RTL writing directions. Set `dir` to `rtl`.\n\nWhen this attribute is set, we attach a `dir` attribute to the root part.\n\n```jsx {2}\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  dir: \"rtl\",\n})\n```\n\n### Submitting with an external form\n\nSet `form` if the hidden input should submit with a form outside the current DOM\nsubtree.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  name: \"value\",\n  form: \"checkout-form\",\n})\n```\n\n### Customizing accessibility labels\n\nUse `translations.inputLabel` to customize screen-reader labels per input.\n\n```jsx\nconst service = useMachine(pinInput.machine, {\n  count: 4,\n  translations: {\n    inputLabel: (index, length) =\u003e `Digit ${index + 1} of ${length}`,\n  },\n})\n```\n\n## Styling guide\n\nEach part includes a `data-part` attribute you can target in CSS.\n\n### Completed state\n\nWhen all values have been filled, we attach a `data-complete` attribute to the\nroot and input parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-complete] {\n  /* styles for when all value has been filled */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-complete] {\n  /* styles for when all value has been filled */\n}\n```\n\n### Invalid state\n\nWhen an invalid value is entered, we attach a `data-invalid` attribute to the\naffected input part.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-invalid] {\n  /* styles for when the input is invalid */\n}\n```\n\n### Disabled state\n\nWhen the pin-input is disabled, we attach a `data-disabled` attribute to the\nroot and input parts.\n\n```css\n[data-part=\"root\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for when the input is disabled */\n}\n\n[data-part=\"input\"][data-disabled] {\n  /* styles for when the input is disabled */\n}\n```\n\n## Methods and Properties\n\n### Machine Context\n\nThe pin input machine exposes the following context properties:\n\n\u003cContextTable name=\"pin-input\" /\u003e\n\n### Machine API\n\nThe pin input `api` exposes the following methods:\n\n\u003cApiTable name=\"pin-input\" /\u003e\n\n### Data Attributes\n\n\u003cDataAttrTable name=\"pin-input\" /\u003e\n\n##
